					Brandenburg Concerto No.3 in G major, BWV 1048 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>

<td>1718
</td></tr>

<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Concertos&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Concertos</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_3_violins%2C_3_violas%2C_3_cellos%2C_continuo&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 3 violins, 3 violas, 3 cellos, continuo</a></span>; <th>Misc. Notes

Bach P 1063</a></span> This manuscript is thought to preserve a version earlier than the final, dedicated version, although the deviation from the final version is rather small.
